## OpenHands Workspace Rules

- The provided working directory is the only submission surface for this evaluation.
- Do not `git clone`, `git init`, or fetch the target repository into the working directory or any of its subdirectories.
- Use MCP to inspect remote code, then create or edit only the files you need directly in the working directory using repository-relative paths.
- The verifier only reads changes from the provided working directory, not from any self-cloned checkout.


# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# big-code-flink-arch-001: Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture

## Task

Map the Flink checkpoint coordination architecture: how the JobManager triggers a checkpoint, propagates barriers through the task graph, and coordinates acknowledgments. Trace the complete distributed two-phase commit from CheckpointCoordinator through barrier injection, barrier alignment/processing at downstream tasks, state snapshot, acknowledgment, to CompletedCheckpoint.

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc (mirror of apache/flink) (Java, ~3.5M LOC)
- **Category**: Architectural Understanding
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: flink-runtime/checkpoint/ and flink-streaming-java/runtime/io/checkpointing/

## Requirements

1. Identify all relevant components in the checkpoint coordination flow (JobManager-side coordinator, RPC dispatch, barrier events, barrier handlers, state snapshot, acknowledgment)
2. Trace the dependency chain from CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint() through barrier propagation to CompletedCheckpoint
3. Document the aligned vs unaligned checkpoint barrier handling (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler vs CheckpointBarrierTracker)
4. Explain the PendingCheckpoint lifecycle and the ack-based completion protocol

## Expected Output

Write your analysis to `/logs/agent/solution.md` with the following structure:

```
## Files Examined
- path/to/file1.ext — role in architecture
- path/to/file2.ext — role in architecture
...

## Dependency Chain
1. Entry point: path/to/entry.ext
2. Calls: path/to/next.ext (via function/method name)
3. Delegates to: path/to/impl.ext
...

## Analysis
[Detailed architectural analysis including:
- Design patterns identified
- Component responsibilities
- Data flow description
- Interface contracts between components]

## Summary
[Concise 2-3 sentence summary answering the task question]
```

## Evaluation Criteria

- File recall: Did you find the correct set of architecturally relevant files?
- Dependency accuracy: Did you trace the correct dependency/call chain?
- Architectural coherence: Did you correctly identify the design patterns and component relationships?

</EFFICIENCY>

## Complete Architecture Flow

### 1. JobManager Side - Trigger Phase

**CheckpointCoordinator** (flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinator.java)
- Entry point: `triggerCheckpoint(boolean isPeriodic)` → `triggerCheckpointFromCheckpointThread()` → `triggerCheckpoint(props, location, isPeriodic)`
- Creates `CheckpointTriggerRequest`, passes to `chooseRequestToExecute()` → `startTriggeringCheckpoint()`
- `startTriggeringCheckpoint()`:
  1. Calls `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` to determine which tasks to trigger/wait for
  2. Gets checkpoint ID from `checkpointIdCounter.getAndIncrement()`
  3. Creates `PendingCheckpoint` via `createPendingCheckpoint()` - registers in `pendingCheckpoints` map, schedules timeout via `CheckpointCanceller`
  4. Initializes checkpoint storage location via `initializeCheckpointLocation()`
  5. Triggers OperatorCoordinator checkpoints via `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion()`
  6. Snapshots master hook states via `snapshotMasterState()`
  7. After all coordinator/master states complete, calls `triggerCheckpointRequest()` → `triggerTasks()`

The analysis is complete. Here's a summary of what I found and documented:

## Summary of Findings

### Complete Checkpoint Coordination Flow

**Phase 1 — Trigger & Barrier Propagation:**
1. `CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()` creates a `PendingCheckpoint`, triggers OperatorCoordinator/master-hook snapshots, then sends `triggerCheckpoint` RPCs to source tasks via `Execution` → `TaskManagerGateway` → `TaskExecutorGateway`
2. Source tasks receive the trigger in `StreamTask`, which calls `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()` — this broadcasts a `CheckpointBarrier` downstream, takes a synchronous state snapshot, and submits an `AsyncCheckpointRunnable`
3. Downstream tasks receive barriers through `CheckpointedInputGate` → `CheckpointBarrierHandler`, which either aligns (blocks channels) or tracks (counts) barriers before triggering their own snapshots

**Phase 2 — Acknowledgment & Completion:**
4. `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` finalizes snapshot futures and calls `TaskStateManagerImpl.reportTaskStateSnapshots()` → `checkpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint()` RPC back to the JobMaster
5. `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()` calls `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()` until `isFullyAcknowledged()`, then `completePendingCheckpoint()` writes metadata, creates `CompletedCheckpoint`, persists to HA store, and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks

### Key Architectural Distinction
- **`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler`** (EXACTLY_ONCE): Uses a `BarrierHandlerState` state machine; blocks channels during alignment; supports aligned, unaligned (immediate trigger + in-flight buffer capture), and alternating (aligned with timeout fallback to unaligned) modes
- **`CheckpointBarrierTracker`** (AT_LEAST_ONCE): Simply counts barriers without b
... (truncated)

JobManager Side - Trigger Phase\n\n**CheckpointCoordinator** (flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinator.java)\n- Entry point: `triggerCheckpoint(boolean isPeriodic)` \u2192 `triggerCheckpointFromCheckpointThread()` \u2192 `triggerCheckpoint(props, location, isPeriodic)`\n- Creates `CheckpointTriggerRequest`, passes to `chooseRequestToExecute()` \u2192 `startTriggeringCheckpoint()`\n- `startTriggeringCheckpoint()`:\n  1. Calls `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` to determine which tasks to trigger/wait for\n  2. Gets checkpoint ID from `checkpointIdCounter.getAndIncrement()`\n  3. Creates `PendingCheckpoint` via `createPendingCheckpoint()` - registers in `pendingCheckpoints` map, schedules timeout via `CheckpointCanceller`\n  4. Initializes checkpoint storage location via `initializeCheckpointLocation()`\n  5. Triggers OperatorCoordinator checkpoints via `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion()`\n  6. Snapshots master hook states via `snapshotMasterState()`\n  7. After all coordinator/master states complete, calls `triggerCheckpointRequest()` \u2192 `triggerTasks()`\n- `triggerTasks()`: For each source task in `checkpoint.getCheckpointPlan().getTasksToTrigger()`, calls `execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`\n\n### 2. RPC Dispatch - Trigger to TaskManager\n\n**Execution** (flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/executiongraph/Execution.java)\n- `triggerCheckpoint()` \u2192 gets `TaskManagerGateway` from slot \u2192 calls `taskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint(attemptId, jobId, checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`\n\n**TaskManagerGateway** (interface) \u2192 **RpcTaskManagerGateway** (implementation)\n- `RpcTaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint()` \u2192 delegates to `TaskExecutorGateway.triggerCheckpoint()` (RPC call to TaskExecutor)\n\n**TaskExecutorGateway** (interface) \u2192 **TaskExecutor** (implementation)\n- Receives RPC, finds the Task, calls `task.triggerCheckpointBarrier(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`\n\n### 3. Task Side - Barrier Injection\n\n**StreamTask** (flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/StreamTask.java)\n- `triggerCheckpointAsync()` \u2192 `performCheckpoint()` \u2192 `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()`\n\n**SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl** (flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java)\n- `checkpointState()` steps:\n  1. `operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier()` - pre-barrier work\n  2. Creates `CheckpointBarrier` and calls `operatorChain.broadcastEvent(checkpointBarrier)` - **injects barrier into output channels**\n  3. Registers alignment timer (for alternating checkpoints)\n  4. For unaligned: `channelStateWriter.finishOutput()` - captures in-flight output buffers\n  5. `takeSnapshotSync()` - synchronous snapshot of operator state via `operatorChain.snapshotState()`\n  6. `finishAndReportAsync()` - submits `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` to async thread pool\n\n### 4. Downstream Task - Barrier Processing\n\n**CheckpointedInputGate** wraps the input gate and routes barrier events to the `CheckpointBarrierHandler`.\n\n**CheckpointBarrierHandler** (abstract base class)\n- `notifyCheckpoint()` \u2192 calls `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` (which is the StreamTask)\n\nTwo implementations:\n\n**CheckpointBarrierTracker** (AT_LEAST_ONCE mode):\n- Does NOT block input channels\n- Tracks barriers per checkpoint ID using `CheckpointBarrierCount` queue\n- When all barriers received for a checkpoint ID \u2192 `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` \u2192 `notifyCheckpoint()`\n- Can track up to 50 concurrent checkpoints\n\n**SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler** (EXACTLY_ONCE mode):\n- Blocks input channels that have sent barriers (alignment)\n- Three factory methods: `aligned()`, `unaligned()`, `alternating()`\n- Uses State Machine pattern via `BarrierHandlerState` interface:\n  - `WaitingForFirstBarrier` \u2192 initial state\n  - `CollectingBarriers` \u2192 aligned, blocking channels\n  - `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier` \u2192 for alternating mode\n  - `AlternatingCollectingBarriers` \u2192 aligned phase of alternating\n  - `AlternatingCollectingBarriersUnaligned` \u2192 unaligned phase\n- `processBarrier()` \u2192 `markCheckpointAlignedAndTransformState()` \u2192 state.barrierReceived()\n- When all channels aligned \u2192 `allBarriersReceivedFuture.complete(null)`\n- For unaligned: `processBarrierAnnouncement()` triggers checkpoint immediately on first announcement\n\n**InputProcessorUtil** selects the handler:\n- EXACTLY_ONCE + unaligned \u2192 `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.alternating()`\n- EXACTLY_ONCE + aligned \u2192 `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned()`\n- AT_LEAST_ONCE \u2192 `CheckpointBarrierTracker`\n\n### 5. State Snapshot\n\nWhen barrier handler triggers checkpoint on the downstream task:\n- `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` \u2192 `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()`\n- `StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` \u2192 `performCheckpoint()` \u2192 `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()`\n- Same flow as source task but without barrier injection (already received barriers)\n\n**AsyncCheckpointRunnable** (flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/AsyncCheckpointRunnable.java):\n- Runs in async thread pool\n- `finalizeNonFinishedSnapshots()` - waits for all `OperatorSnapshotFutures` to complete\n- `reportCompletedSnapshotStates()` \u2192 `taskEnvironment.getTaskStateManager().reportTaskStateSnapshots()`\n\n### 6. Acknowledgment - Task to JobManager\n\n**TaskStateManagerImpl** (flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/state/TaskStateManagerImpl.java):\n- `reportTaskStateSnapshots()` \u2192 `checkpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint(jobId, executionAttemptID, checkpointId, checkpointMetrics, acknowledgedState)`\n\n**CheckpointCoordinatorGateway** (RPC interface):\n- `acknowledgeCheckpoint()` - RPC call back to JobMaster\n\n**JobMaster** \u2192 **CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()**:\n- Looks up `PendingCheckpoint` by checkpoint ID\n- Calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionAttemptId, subtaskState, metrics)`\n- `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()` removes task from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks`\n- If `checkpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` \u2192 `completePendingCheckpoint()`\n\n### 7. Completion - PendingCheckpoint \u2192 CompletedCheckpoint\n\n**CheckpointCoordinator.completePendingCheckpoint()**:\n1. `finalizeCheckpoint()` \u2192 `pendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint()`:\n   - Writes checkpoint metadata via `Checkpoints.storeCheckpointMetadata()`\n   - Creates `CompletedCheckpoint` object\n2. `addCompletedCheckpointToStoreAndSubsumeOldest()` \u2192 `completedCheckpointStore.addCheckpointAndSubsumeOldestOne()`\n3. `reportCompletedCheckpoint()` - updates stats\n4. `pendingCheckpoint.getCompletionFuture().complete(completedCheckpoint)` - fulfills the original trigger future\n5. `cleanupAfterCompletedCheckpoint()` \u2192 `sendAcknowledgeMessages()` - notifies all tasks of completion via `execution.notifyCheckpointOnComplete()`\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle\n\n1. **Created**: `createPendingCheckpoint()` - registered in `pendingCheckpoints` map, timeout scheduled\n2. **Waiting**: Tracks `notYetAcknowledgedTasks`, `notYetAcknowledgedOperatorCoordinators`, `notYetAcknowledgedMasterStates`\n3. **Acknowledging**: Each `acknowledgeTask()` call removes from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks`\n4. **Fully Acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = all three sets empty\n5. **Finalized**: `finalizeCheckpoint()` writes metadata, creates `CompletedCheckpoint`, marks as disposed\n6. **Completed**: `onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)` - future fulfilled\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n1. **Two-Phase Commit**: Phase 1 = barrier propagation + state snapshot + ack; Phase 2 = coordinator sends \"notify complete\" to all tasks\n2. **State Machine**: `BarrierHandlerState` for barrier alignment in `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler`\n3. **Observer/Listener**: `CheckpointableTask` interface notified by `CheckpointBarrierHandler`\n4. **Gateway/RPC**: `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`, `TaskManagerGateway`, `TaskExecutorGateway` for distributed communication\n5. **Future-based async**: `CompletableFuture` chains throughout coordinator\n6. **Template Method**: `CheckpointBarrierHandler` abstract class with concrete implementations\n"

`AsyncCheckpointRunnable.java`\n\n15. **ACK sent to JobMaster**: `TaskStateManagerImpl.reportTaskStateSnapshots()`:\n    - `localStateStore.storeLocalState(checkpointId, localState)` \u2014 stores local state copy\n    - `checkpointResponder.acknowledgeCheckpoint(jobId, executionAttemptID, checkpointId, metrics, acknowledgedState)` \u2014 RPC call via `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`\n    - File: `TaskStateManagerImpl.java`, `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway.java`\n\n16. **ACK received at coordinator**: `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage(AcknowledgeCheckpoint)`:\n    - Looks up `PendingCheckpoint` by checkpoint ID\n    - `checkpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionAttemptId, subtaskState, metrics)` \u2192 removes task from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks`, stores `OperatorSubtaskState`\n    - If `checkpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` \u2192 `completePendingCheckpoint(checkpoint)`\n    - File: `CheckpointCoordinator.java`, `PendingCheckpoint.java`\n\n17. **Checkpoint completion**: `completePendingCheckpoint(pendingCheckpoint)`:\n    - `finalizeCheckpoint(pendingCheckpoint)` \u2192 `pendingCheckpoint.finalizeCheckpoint(...)`:\n      - Writes `CheckpointMetadata` via `Checkpoints.storeCheckpointMetadata(savepoint, out)`\n      - Creates `CompletedCheckpoint` with all operator states and finalized storage location\n    - `addCompletedCheckpointToStoreAndSubsumeOldest(...)` \u2192 `completedCheckpointStore.addCheckpointAndSubsumeOldestOne(...)` \u2014 persists to HA store, subsumes older checkpoints\n    - `reportCompletedCheckpoint(completedCheckpoint)` \u2014 updates stats tracker\n    - `pendingCheckpoint.getCompletionFuture().complete(completedCheckpoint)` \u2014 fulfills the original trigger future\n    - `cleanupAfterCompletedCheckpoint(...)` \u2192 `sendAcknowledgeMessages(...)` \u2014 notifies all tasks via `execution.notifyCheckpointOnComplete()` (RPC) and all OperatorCoordinators\n    - File: `CheckpointCoordinator.java`, `PendingCheckpoint.java`, `CompletedCheckpoint.java`\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**1. Distributed Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**\n\nFlink's checkpoint protocol is a distributed 2PC:\n- **Phase 1 (Prepare/Vote)**: The coordinator triggers barriers; each task takes a state snapshot and sends an `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` message (its \"vote to commit\"). The `PendingCheckpoint` accumulates these votes.\n- **Phase 2 (Commit)**: Once all tasks have acknowledged (`isFullyAcknowledged()`), the coordinator finalizes the checkpoint metadata, persists it to the `CompletedCheckpointStore`, and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks. Tasks then call `notifyCheckpointComplete` on their operators (e.g., Kafka consumer commits offsets).\n\n**2. State Machine for Barrier Alignment**\n\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` uses the State pattern (`BarrierHandlerState` interface) to manage the complex lifecycle of barrier alignment:\n- `WaitingForFirstBarrier` \u2192 `CollectingBarriers` (aligned mode)\n- `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier` \u2192 `AlternatingCollectingBarriers` \u2192 `AlternatingCollectingBarriersUnaligned` (alternating mode, can time out from aligned to unaligned)\n- `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned` \u2192 `AlternatingCollectingBarriersUnaligned` (strict unaligned mode)\n\nState transitions are triggered by `barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, `alignedCheckpointTimeout()`, and `abort()`.\n\n**3. Observer/Listener Pattern**\n\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds a reference to `CheckpointableTask` (implemented by `StreamTask`). When all barriers are received, it calls `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()`, decoupling barrier tracking from checkpoint execution.\n\n**4. Gateway/RPC Abstraction**\n\nThree gateway layers separate concerns:\n- `TaskManagerGateway` (JobManager\u2192TaskManager): `triggerCheckpoint`, `abortCheckpoint`\n- `TaskExecutorGateway` (same, RPC-level): implemented by Pekko/Akka actors\n- `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway` (TaskManager\u2192JobManager): `acknowledgeCheckpoint`, `declineCheckpoint`\n\n**5. Future-Based Async Pipeline**\n\n`CheckpointCoordinator.startTriggeringCheckpoint()` chains `CompletableFuture` stages: plan calculation \u2192 ID allocation \u2192 pending checkpoint creation \u2192 storage location init \u2192 coordinator checkpoints \u2192 master hooks \u2192 task trigger. This avoids blocking the coordinator thread on I/O.\n\n**6. Template Method**\n\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` defines the algorithm skeleton (`notifyCheckpoint`, `notifyAbort`, alignment tracking) while subclasses (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler`, `CheckpointBarrierTracker`) implement the barrier processing logic.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|-----------|---------------|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Orchestrates the entire checkpoint lifecycle: trigger, track, complete, abort |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable in-flight state; accumulates task ACKs; finalizes to `CompletedCheckpoint` |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record of a successful checkpoint; persisted to HA store |\n| `CheckpointPlanCalculator` | Determines which tasks to trigger vs. wait for based on topology |\n| `Execution` | Dispatches trigger RPC to the TaskManager for a specific task attempt |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-side: broadcasts barrier, takes snapshot, submits async finalization |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Finalizes async snapshot futures; sends ACK via `TaskStateManagerImpl` |\n| `TaskStateManagerImpl` | Bridges task to coordinator: stores local state, sends `acknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Intercepts barrier events from the network layer |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | EXACTLY_ONCE barrier alignment with channel blocking and state machine |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | AT_LEAST_ONCE barrier counting without channel blocking |\n| `InputProcessorUtil` | Factory selecting the correct barrier handler based on configuration |\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n```\nJobManager (CheckpointCoordinator)\n  \u2502\n  \u251c\u2500 1. Calculate plan (which tasks to trigger/wait for)\n  \u251c\u2500 2. Allocate checkpoint ID\n  \u251c\u2500 3. Create PendingCheckpoint (register in map, schedule timeout)\n  \u251c\u2500 4. Initialize storage location\n  \u251c\u2500 5. Trigger OperatorCoordinator checkpoints (async)\n  \u251c\u2500 6. Trigger master hook snapshots (async)\n  \u2514\u2500 7. Broadcast CheckpointBarrier to output channels \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n  \u251c\u2500 10. [Unaligned] Capture in-flight output buffers                        \u2502\n  \u251c\u2500 11. takeSnapshotSync (operator state)                                   \u2502\n  \u2514\u2500 12. Submit AsyncCheckpointRunnable                                      \u2502\n           \u2502                                                                  \u2502\n           \u25bc     \u251c\u2500 complete onCompletionPromise\n       \u2514\u2500 sendAcknowledgeMessages() \u2192 notifyCheckpointOnComplete RPC to all tasks\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n- **`CheckpointCoordinator` \u2194 `PendingCheckpoint`**: Coordinator creates and owns `PendingCheckpoint`; calls `acknowledgeTask()`, `isFullyAcknowledged()`, `finalizeCheckpoint()`. `PendingCheckpoint` is `@NotThreadSafe` and must be accessed under the coordinator's `lock`.\n- **`CheckpointBarrierHandler` \u2194 `CheckpointableTask`**: Handler calls `triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` and `abortCheckpointOnBarrier()` on the task. The task must not block these calls.\n- **`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` \u2194 `OperatorChain`**: Coordinator calls `prepareSnapshotPreBarrier()`, `broadcastEvent()`, `snapshotState()` on the chain. The chain iterates operators in reverse order for snapshots.\n- **`AsyncCheckpointRunnable` \u2194 `TaskStateManagerImpl`**: Runnable calls `reportTaskStateSnapshots()` with the finalized `TaskStateSnapshot`. `TaskStateManagerImpl` is responsible for the RPC call.\n- **`TaskStateManagerImpl` \u2194 `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`**: `acknowledgeCheckpoint()` is a fire-and-forget RPC; the coordinator processes it asynchronously.\n\n### Aligned vs. Unaligned Checkpoint Handling\n\n**Aligned (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned()`)**:\n- Initial state: `WaitingForFirstBarrier`\n- On first barrier: transitions to `CollectingBarriers`, blocks the channel that sent the barrier\n- On subsequent barriers: blocks each channel, counts aligned channels\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: triggers checkpoint, unblocks all channels\n- Guarantees exactly-once by ensuring no records from after the barrier are processed before the snapshot\n- Drawback: can cause back-pressure if one channel is slow\n\n**Unaligned (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.unaligned()`)**:\n- Initial state: `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`\n- On first barrier announcement (`processBarrierAnnouncement()`): immediately triggers checkpoint\n- Captures in-flight buffers in all channels (input and output) as part of checkpoint state\n- Does NOT block channels; processing continues while snapshot is taken\n- Eliminates alignment back-pressure at the cost of larger checkpoint size\n\n**Alternating (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.alternating()`)**:\n- Starts in aligned mode (`AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier`)\n- If alignment completes within `alignedCheckpointTimeout`: stays aligned\n- If timeout fires (`alignedCheckpointTimeout()` on state): transitions to `AlternatingCollectingBarriersUnaligned`, switches to unaligned mode mid-checkpoint\n- Balances latency (aligned when fast) with throughput (unaligned when slow)\n\n**`CheckpointBarrierTracker` (AT_LEAST_ONCE)**:\n- Maintains a queue of `CheckpointBarrierCount` objects (up to 50)\n- Does NOT block any channels; records continue flowing\n- Ignores `processBarrierAnnouncement()` entirely\n- When all channels counted for a checkpoint ID: triggers checkpoint\n- Older checkpoints are subsumed when a newer one completes\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink's checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit protocol driven by the `CheckpointCoordinator` on the JobManager. In Phase 1, the coordinator creates a `PendingCheckpoint`, triggers source tasks via RPC (`Execution` \u2192 `TaskManagerGateway` \u2192 `TaskExecutorGateway`), and each source task injects a `CheckpointBarrier` into its output channels via `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()`; downstream tasks receive barriers through `CheckpointedInputGate` and either align them (blocking channels until all barriers arrive, via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler`) or simply count them (via `CheckpointBarrierTracker`), then take their own state snapshots and send `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPCs back to the coordinator via `TaskStateManagerImpl`. In Phase 2, once `PendingCheckpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` is true (all tasks, OperatorCoordinators, and master hooks have acknowledged), the coordinator calls `finalizeCheckpoint()` to write metadata and create a `CompletedCheckpoint`, persists it to the `CompletedCheckpointStore`, and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks so they can commit external side effects (e.g., Kafka offsets). The aligned vs. unaligned distinction is encapsulated in the `BarrierHandlerState` state machine within `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler`, where aligned mode blocks channels to prevent out-of-order processing, unaligned mode captures in-flight buffers and triggers immediately on the first barrier announcement, and alternating mode starts aligned but can time out to unaligned to avoid back-pressure.\n",
